I asked the front desk to give me a room on a high floor, where I could see the sea. The hotel faces due west, so if the weather is good, I should be able to see the sunset, but it has been raining for the past two days. The room has good light blocking, so it won't affect sleeping during the day.
For breakfast, it is a semi-self-service and semi-ordering method. The dining environment is very comfortable, the space is very open, and the waiter's service is very timely. It is great to remember the guests. The existing dishes taste good, and it would be better if the dishes every day could be more diverse.
Although there were some minor episodes during the check-in process, the hotel was able to handle the problem in time at five in the morning, which was very good (it was that there was no more after the problem was handled. It would be more comfortable if I could take the initiative to make a return call or communicate to give some small compensation, but the overall solution process was still very smooth)
Finally, the sound insulation of the hotel room door is not good. It should be the biggest flaw of the hotel. I can hear the sound of people walking and talking in the corridor. I hope it can be improved in the future.
Overall, this hotel can be called the ceiling of Conrad in China. Both the interior and exterior design of the hotel and the check-in experience are very good. I will choose it again when I come to Shenzhen in the future. Finally, thank you Bani. The return visit was very timely after checking out. The voice was nice haha.
